a/src/widgets/block.zig b/src/widgets/block.zig\nnew file mode 100644\nindex 0000000..fdf755f\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/src/widgets/block.zig\n@@ -0,0 +1,498 @@\n+// Block widget for zithril TUI framework\n+// Draws borders and optional title\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+const text_mod = @import(\"text.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+pub const Alignment = text_mod.Alignment;\n+\n+/// Border style variants\n+pub const BorderType = enum {\n+    none,\n+    plain, // ASCII: +-|\n+    rounded, // Unicode: rounded corners\n+    double, // Unicode: double lines\n+    thick, // Unicode: thick lines\n+\n+    /// Get the border character set for this border type\n+    pub fn chars(self: BorderType) BorderChars {\n+        return switch (self) {\n+            .none => BorderChars{\n+                .top_left = ' ',\n+                .top_right = ' ',\n+                .bottom_left = ' ',\n+                .bottom_right = ' ',\n+                .horizontal = ' ',\n+                .vertical = ' ',\n+            },\n+            .plain => BorderChars{\n+                .top_left = '+',\n+                .top_right = '+',\n+                .bottom_left = '+',\n+                .bottom_right = '+',\n+                .horizontal = '-',\n+                .vertical = '|',\n+            },\n+            .rounded => BorderChars{\n+                .top_left = 0x256D, // Box Drawings Light Arc Down and Right\n+                .top_right = 0x256E, // Box Drawings Light Arc Down and Left\n+                .bottom_left = 0x2570, // Box Drawings Light Arc Up and Right\n+                .bottom_right = 0x256F, // Box Drawings Light Arc Up and Left\n+                .horizontal = 0x2500, // Box Drawings Light Horizontal\n+                .vertical = 0x2502, // Box Drawings Light Vertical\n+            },\n+            .double => BorderChars{\n+                .top_left = 0x2554, // Box Drawings Double Down and Right\n+                .top_right = 0x2557, // Box Drawings Double Down and Left\n+                .bottom_left = 0x255A, // Box Drawings Double Up and Right\n+                .bottom_right = 0x255D, // Box Drawings Double Up and Left\n+                .horizontal = 0x2550, // Box Drawings Double Horizontal\n+                .vertical = 0x2551, // Box Drawings Double Vertical\n+            },\n+            .thick => BorderChars{\n+                .top_left = 0x250F, // Box Drawings Heavy Down and Right\n+                .top_right = 0x2513, // Box Drawings Heavy Down and Left\n+                .bottom_left = 0x2517, // Box Drawings Heavy Up and Right\n+                .bottom_right = 0x251B, // Box Drawings Heavy Up and Left\n+                .horizontal = 0x2501, // Box Drawings Heavy Horizontal\n+                .vertical = 0x2503, // Box Drawings Heavy Vertical\n+            },\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Character set for drawing borders\n+pub const BorderChars = struct {\n+    top_left: u21,\n+    top_right: u21,\n+    bottom_left: u21,\n+    bottom_right: u21,\n+    horizontal: u21,\n+    vertical: u21,\n+};\n+\n+/// Block widget that draws borders and optional title.\n+/// Use inner() on the Rect to get the interior area for child content.\n+pub const Block = struct {\n+    /// Optional title displayed at the top of the block\n+    title: ?[]const u8 = null,\n+\n+    /// Alignment of the title within the top border\n+    title_alignment: Alignment = .left,\n+\n+    /// Border style (none, plain, rounded, double, thick)\n+    border: BorderType = .none,\n+\n+    /// Style applied to border characters\n+    border_style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Background style applied to the interior of the block\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Render the block into the buffer at the given area.\n+    /// Draws the border and title, fills interior with background style.\n+    pub fn render(self: Block, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        // Fill interior with background style if we have one\n+        if (!self.style.isEmpty()) {\n+            const fill_cell = Cell.styled(' ', self.style);\n+            buf.fill(area, fill_cell);\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw border if we have one\n+        if (self.border != .none) {\n+            self.drawBorder(area, buf);\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw title if we have one\n+        if (self.title) |title| {\n+            self.drawTitle(title, area, buf);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Draw the border around the area\n+    fn drawBorder(self: Block, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        const chars = self.border.chars();\n+        const style = self.border_style;\n+\n+        const left = area.x;\n+        const right = area.right() -| 1;\n+        const top = area.y;\n+        const bottom_y = area.bottom() -| 1;\n+\n+        // Draw corners\n+        buf.set(left, top, Cell.styled(chars.top_left, style));\n+\n+        if (area.width > 1) {\n+            buf.set(right, top, Cell.styled(chars.top_right, style));\n+        }\n+\n+        if (area.height > 1) {\n+            buf.set(left, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.bottom_left, style));\n+\n+            if (area.width > 1) {\n+                buf.set(right, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.bottom_right, style));\n+            }\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw horizontal lines (top and bottom)\n+        if (area.width > 2) {\n+            const draw_bottom = area.height > 1;\n+            var x = left + 1;\n+            while (x < right) : (x += 1) {\n+                buf.set(x, top, Cell.styled(chars.horizontal, style));\n+                if (draw_bottom) {\n+                    buf.set(x, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.horizontal, style));\n+                }\n+            }\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw vertical lines (left and right sides)\n+        if (area.height > 2) {\n+            const draw_right = area.width > 1;\n+            var y = top + 1;\n+            while (y < bottom_y) : (y += 1) {\n+                buf.set(left, y, Cell.styled(chars.vertical, style));\n+                if (draw_right) {\n+                    buf.set(right, y, Cell.styled(chars.vertical, style));\n+                }\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Draw the title in the top border\n+    fn drawTitle(self: Block, title: []const u8, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        // Need at least 3 width to show any title (border + 1 char + border)\n+        if (area.width < 3) return;\n+\n+        // Calculate available space for title (inside the corners)\n+        const available_width = area.width - 2;\n+        const title_len = @min(available_width, @as(u16, @intCast(title.len)));\n+\n+        // Calculate x position based on alignment\n+        const title_x: u16 = switch (self.title_alignment) {\n+            .left => area.x + 1,\n+            .center => area.x + 1 + (available_width -| title_len) / 2,\n+            .right => area.x + 1 + (available_width -| title_len),\n+        };\n+\n+        // Draw the title with border style (title inherits border style)\n+        buf.setString(title_x, area.y, title[0..title_len], self.border_style);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the interior area (inside the border).\n+    /// Returns a Rect with margin 1 if there's a border, otherwise the full area.\n+    pub fn inner(self: Block, area: Rect) Rect {\n+        if (self.border == .none) {\n+            return area;\n+        }\n+        return area.inner(1);\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic Block functionality\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: Block with default values\" {\n+    const block = Block{};\n+    try std.testing.expect(block.title == null);\n+    try std.testing.expect(block.border == .none);\n+    try std.testing.expect(block.style.isEmpty());\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Block with title and border\" {\n+    const block = Block{\n+        .title = \"Test\",\n+        .border = .rounded,\n+    };\n+    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Test\", block.title.?);\n+    try std.testing.expect(block.border == .rounded);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Block.inner returns correct interior area\" {\n+    const block = Block{ .border = .plain };\n+    const area = Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 10);\n+    const interior = block.inner(area);\n+\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 1), interior.x);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 1), interior.y);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 18), interior.width);\n+    try std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+pub const Color = style_mod.Color;\n+\n+/// Navigable list widget with items, selection highlighting, and scroll support.\n+///\n+/// Renders a vertical list of text items. The selected item is highlighted\n+/// with highlight_style and prefixed with highlight_symbol.\n+pub const List = struct {\n+    /// The items to display in the list\n+    items: []const []const u8,\n+\n+    /// Currently selected item index (null for no selection)\n+    selected: ?usize = null,\n+\n+    /// Default style for non-selected items\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Style for the selected item\n+    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n+\n+    /// Prefix shown before the selected item\n+    highlight_symbol: []const u8 = \"> \",\n+\n+    /// Render the list into the buffer at the given area.\n+    /// Each item takes one row. Items beyond the area height are not rendered.\n+    pub fn render(self: List, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n+\n+        const symbol_len: u16 = @intCast(@min(self.highlight_symbol.len, area.width));\n+        const content_start = area.x +| symbol_len;\n+        const content_width = area.width -| symbol_len;\n+\n+        // Render visible items\n+        var y = area.y;\n+        var item_index: usize = 0;\n+        while (item_index < self.items.len and y < area.bottom()) : ({\n+            y += 1;\n+            item_index += 1;\n+        }) {\n+            const item = self.items[item_index];\n+            const is_selected = self.selected != null and self.selected.? == item_index;\n+\n+            if (is_selected) {\n+                // Fill the entire row with highlight style\n+                const row_rect = Rect.init(area.x, y, area.width, 1);\n+                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n+\n+                // Draw highlight symbol\n+                if (symbol_len > 0) {\n+                    buf.setString(area.x, y, self.highlight_symbol[0..symbol_len], self.highlight_style);\n+                }\n+\n+                // Draw item text with highlight style\n+                if (content_width > 0) {\n+                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.highlight_style);\n+                }\n+            } else {\n+                // Draw item text with normal style (offset for alignment with highlighted items)\n+                if (content_width > 0) {\n+                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.style);\n+                }\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the number of items in the list\n+    pub fn len(self: List) usize {\n+        return self.items.len;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if the list is empty\n+    pub fn isEmpty(self: List) bool {\n+        return self.items.len == 0;\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic List functionality\n+// 0000000..6bc48e0\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/src/widgets/text.zig\n@@ -0,0 +1,267 @@\n+// Text widget for zithril TUI framework\n+// Single-line styled text with alignment\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+\n+/// Text alignment options\n+pub const Alignment = enum {\n+    left,\n+    center,\n+    right,\n+};\n+\n+/// Single-line styled text widget.\n+///\n+/// Renders text content with a given style and alignment within the provided area.\n+/// Text is clipped if it exceeds the available width. Only renders on the first\n+/// row of the area (single-line).\n+pub const Text = struct {\n+    /// The text content to display\n+    content: []const u8,\n+\n+    /// Style applied to the text\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Text alignment within the area\n+    alignment: Alignment = .left,\n+\n+    /// Render the text into the buffer at the given area.\n+    /// Only uses the first row of the area. Text is clipped at area boundaries.\n+    pub fn render(self: Text, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+        if (self.content.len == 0) return;\n+\n+        // Calculate visible text length (capped by area width)\n+        const text_len = textDisplayWidth(self.content);\n+        const visible_len = @min(text_len, area.width);\n+\n+        if (visible_len == 0) return;\n+\n+        // Calculate x position based on alignment\n+        const x_offset: u16 = switch (self.alignment) {\n+            .left => 0,\n+            .center => (area.width -| visible_len) / 2,\n+            .right => area.width -| visible_len,\n+        };\n+\n+        const x = area.x +| x_offset;\n+\n+        // Write the text (setString handles clipping)\n+        buf.setString(x, area.y, self.content, self.style);\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Calculate the display width of a string (counting grapheme columns).\n+/// Simple implementation: counts codepoints, treating wide chars as width 2.\n+fn textDisplayWidth(str: []const u8) u16 {\n+    var width: u16 = 0;\n+    var iter = std.unicode.Utf8View.initUnchecked(str).iterator();\n+    while (iter.nextCodepoint()) |cp| {\n+        width +|= if (isWideCodepoint(cp)) 2 else 1;\n+    }\n+    return width;\n+}\n+\n+/// Check if a codepoint is a wide character (CJK, etc.)\n+fn isWideCodepoint(cp: u21) bool {\n+    // CJK ranges (simplified)\n+    return (cp >= 0x4E00 and cp <= 0x9FFF) or // CJK Unified Ideographs\n+        (cp >= 0x3400 and cp <= 0x4DBF) or // CJK Extension A\n+        (cp >= 0x20000 and cp <= 0x2A6DF) or // CJK Extension B\n+        (cp >= 0xF900 and cp <= 0xFAFF) or // CJK Compatibility\n+        (cp >= 0xFF00 and cp <= 0xFF60) or // Fullwidth forms\n+        (cp >= 0xFFE0 and cp <= 0xFFE6) or // Fullwidth symbols\n+        (cp >= 0x3000 and cp <= 0x303F) or // CJK Punctuation\n+        (cp >= 0x1100 and cp <= 0x11FF); // Hangul Jamo\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic Text functionality\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: Text with default values\" {\n+    const text = Text{ .content = \"Hello\" };\n+    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Hello\", text.content);\n+    try std.testing.expect(text.style.isEmpty());\n+    try std.testing.expect(text.alignment == .left);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Text with custom style\" {\n+    const text = Text{\n+        .content = \"Styled\",\n+        .style = Style.init().bold().fg(.red),\n+    };\n+    try std.testing.expect(text.style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Text with alignment\" {\n+    const left = Text{ .content = \"L\", .alignment = .left };\n+    const center = Text{ .content = \"C\", .alignment = .center };\n+    const right = Text{ .content = \"R\", .alignment = .right };\n+\n+    try std.testing.expect(left.alignment == .left);\n+    try std.testing.expect(center.alignment == .center);\n+    try std.testing.expect(right.alignment == .right);\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Rendering\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text renders left-aligned\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{ .content = \"Hello\", .alignment = .left };\n+    text.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'H'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'e'), buf.get(1, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), buf.get(2, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), buf.get(3, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'o'), buf.get(4, 0).char);\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text renders center-aligned\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{ .content = \"Hi\", .alignment = .center };\n+    text.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    // \"Hi\" (2 chars) centered in 20 = offset 9\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'H'), buf.get(9, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'i'), buf.get(10, 0).char);\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text renders right-aligned\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{ .content = \"End\", .alignment = .right };\n+    text.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    // \"End\" (3 chars) right-aligned in 20 = starts at 17\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'E'), buf.get(17, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'n'), buf.get(18, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'd'), buf.get(19, 0).char);\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text applies style\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{\n+        .content = \"Bold\",\n+        .style = Style.init().bold(),\n+    };\n+    text.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    try std.testing.expect(buf.get(0, 0).style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n+    try std.testing.expect(buf.get(1, 0).style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n+    try std.testing.expect(buf.get(2, 0).style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n+    try std.testing.expect(buf.get(3, 0).style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text renders at area offset\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 30, 10);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{ .content = \"Offset\" };\n+    text.render(Rect.init(5, 3, 10, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'O'), buf.get(5, 3).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'f'), buf.get(6, 3).char);\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text clips long content\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 10, 3);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{ @import(\"text.zig\");\n   105+\n   106+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n   107+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n   108+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n   109+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n   110+pub const Alignment = text_mod.Alignment;\n   111+\n   112+/// Border style variants\n   113+pub const BorderType = enum {\n   114+    none,\n   115+    plain, // ASCII: +-|\n   116+    rounded, // Unicode: rounded corners\n   117+    double, // Unicode: double lines\n   118+    thick, // Unicode: thick lines\n   119+\n   120+    /// Get the border character set for this border type\n   121+    pub fn chars(self: BorderType) BorderChars {\n   122+        return switch (self) {\n   123+            .none => BorderChars{\n   124+                .top_left = ' ',\n   125+                .top_right = ' ',\n   126+                .bottom_left = ' ',\n   127+                .bottom_right = ' ',\n   128+                .horizontal = ' ',\n   129+                .vertical = ' ',\n   130+            },\n   131+            .plain => BorderChars{\n   132+                .top_left = '+',\n   133+                .top_right = '+',\n   134+                .bottom_left = '+',\n   135+                .bottom_right = '+',\n   136+                .horizontal = '-',\n   137+                .vertical = '|',\n   138+            },\n   139+            .rounded => BorderChars{\n   140+                .top_left = 0x256D, // Box Drawings Light Arc Down and Right\n   141+                .top_right = 0x256E, // Box Drawings Light Arc Down and Left\n   142+                .bottom_left = 0x2570, // Box Drawings Light Arc Up and Right\n   143+                .bottom_right = 0x256F, // Box Drawings Light Arc Up and Left\n   144+                .horizontal = 0x2500, // Box Drawings Light Horizontal\n   145+                .vertical = 0x2502, // Box Drawings Light Vertical\n   146+            },\n   147+            .double => BorderChars{\n   148+                .top_left = 0x2554, // Box Drawings Double Down and Right\n   149+                .top_right = 0x2557, // Box Drawings Double Down and Left\n   150+                .bottom_left = 0x255A, // Box Drawings Double Up and Right\n   151+                .bottom_right = 0x255D, // Box Drawings Double Up and Left\n   152+                .horizontal = 0x2550, // Box Drawings Double Horizontal\n   153+                .vertical = 0x2551, // Box Drawings Double Vertical\n   154+            },\n   155+            .thick => BorderChars{\n   156+                .top_left = 0x250F, // Box Drawings Heavy Down and Right\n   157+                .top_right = 0x2513, // Box Drawings Heavy Down and Left\n   158+                .bottom_left = 0x2517, // Box Drawings Heavy Up and Right\n   159+                .bottom_right = 0x251B, // Box Drawings Heavy Up and Left\n   160+                .horizontal = 0x2501, // Box Drawings Heavy Horizontal\n   161+                .vertical = 0x2503, // Box Drawings Heavy Vertical\n   162+            },\n   163+        };\n   164+    }\n   165+};\n   166+\n   167+/// Character set for drawing borders\n   168+pub const BorderChars = struct {\n   169+    top_left: u21,\n   170+    top_right: u21,\n   171+    bottom_left: u21,\n   172+    bottom_right: u21,\n   173+    horizontal: u21,\n   174+    vertical: u21,\n   175+};\n   176+\n   177+/// Block widget that draws borders and optional title.\n   178+/// Use inner() on the Rect to get the interior area for child content.\n   179+pub const Block = struct {\n   180+    /// Optional title displayed at the top of the block\n   181+    title: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   182+\n   183+    /// Alignment of the title within the top border\n   184+    title_alignment: Alignment = .left,\n   185+\n   186+    /// Border style (none, plain, rounded, double, thick)\n   187+    border: BorderType = .none,\n   188+\n   189+    /// Style applied to border characters\n   190+    border_style: Style = Style.empty,\n   191+\n   192+    /// Background style applied to the interior of the block\n   193+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n   194+\n   195+    /// Render the block into the buffer at the given area.\n   196+    /// Draws the border and title, fills interior with background style.\n   197+    pub fn render(self: Block, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   198+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n   199+\n   200+        // Fill interior with background style if we have one\n   201+        if (!self.style.isEmpty()) {\n   202+            const fill_cell = Cell.styled(' ', self.style);\n   203+            buf.fill(area, fill_cell);\n   204+        }\n   205+\n   206+        // Draw border if we have one\n   207+        if (self.border != .none) {\n   208+            self.drawBorder(area, buf);\n   209+        }\n   210+\n   211+        // Draw title if we have one\n   212+        if (self.title) |title| {\n   213+            self.drawTitle(title, area, buf);\n   214+        }\n   215+    }\n   216+\n   217+    /// Draw the border around the area\n   218+    fn drawBorder(self: Block, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   219+        const chars = self.border.chars();\n   220+        const style = self.border_style;\n   221+\n   222+        const left = area.x;\n   223+        const right = area.right() -| 1;\n   224+        const top = area.y;\n   225+        const bottom_y = area.bottom() -| 1;\n   226+\n   227+        // Draw corners\n   228+        buf.set(left, top, Cell.styled(chars.top_left, style));\n   229+\n   230+        if (area.width > 1) {\n   231+            buf.set(right, top, Cell.styled(chars.top_right, style));\n   232+        }\n   233+\n   234+        if (area.height > 1) {\n   235+            buf.set(left, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.bottom_left, style));\n   236+\n   237+            if (area.width > 1) {\n   238+                buf.set(right, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.bottom_right, style));\n   239+            }\n   240+        }\n   241+\n   242+        // Draw horizontal lines (top and bottom)\n   243+        if (area.width > 2) {\n   244+            const draw_bottom = area.height > 1;\n   245+            var x = left + 1;\n   246+            while (x < right) : (x += 1) {\n   247+                buf.set(x, top, Cell.styled(chars.horizontal, style));\n   248+                if (draw_bottom) {\n   249+                    buf.set(x, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.horizontal, style));\n   250+                }\n   251+            }\n   252+        }\n   253+\n   254+        // Draw vertical lines (left and right sides)\n   255+        if (area.height > 2) {\n   256+            const draw_right = area.width > 1;\n   257+            var y = top + 1;\n   258+            while (y < bottom_y) : (y += 1) {\n   259+                buf.set(left, y, Cell.styled(chars.vertical, style));\n   260+                if (draw_right) {\n   261+                    buf.set(right, y, Cell.styled(chars.vertical, style));\n   262+                }\n   263+            }\n   264+        }\n   265+    }\n   266+\n   267+    /// Draw the title in the top border\n   268+    fn drawTitle(self: Block, title: []const u8, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   269+        // Need at least 3 width to show any title (border + 1 char + border)\n   270+        if (area.width < 3) return;\n   271+\n   272+        // Calculate available space for title (inside the corners)\n   273+        const available_width = area.width - 2;\n   274+        const title_len = @min(available_width, @as(u16, @intCast(title.len)));\n   275+\n   276+        // Calculate x position based on alignment\n   277+        const title_x: u16 = switch (self.title_alignment) {\n   278+            .left => area.x + 1,\n   279+            .center => area.x + 1 + (available_width -| title_len) / 2,\n   280+            .right => area.x + 1 + (available_width -| title_len),\n   281+        };\n   282+\n   283+        // Draw the title with border style (title inherits border style)\n   284+        buf.setString(title_x, area.y, title[0..title_len], self.border_style);\n   285+    }\n   286+\n   287+    /// Get the interior area (inside the border).\n   288+    /// Returns a Rect with margin 1 if there's a border, otherwise the full area.\n   289+    pub fn inner(self: Block, area: Rect) Rect {\n   290+        if (self.border == .none) {\n   291+            return area;\n   292+        }\n   293+        return area.inner(1);\n   294+    }\n   295+};\n   296+\n   297+// ============================================================\n   298+// SANITY +1,364 @@\n   601+// List widget for zithril TUI framework\n   602+// Navigable list with items, selection, and highlight styling\n   603+\n   604+const std = @import(\"std\");\n   605+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n   606+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n   607+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n   608+\n   609+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n   610+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n   611+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n   612+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n   613+pub const Color = style_mod.Color;\n   614+\n   615+/// Navigable list widget with items, selection highlighting, and scroll support.\n   616+///\n   617+/// Renders a vertical list of text items. The selected item is highlighted\n   618+/// with highlight_style and prefixed with highlight_symbol.\n   619+pub const List = struct {\n   620+    /// The items to display in the list\n   621+    items: []const []const u8,\n   622+\n   623+    /// Currently selected item index (null for no selection)\n   624+    selected: ?usize = null,\n   625+\n   626+    /// Default style for non-selected items\n   627+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n   628+\n   629+    /// Style for the selected item\n   630+    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n   631+\n   632+    /// Prefix shown before the selected item\n   633+    highlight_symbol: []const u8 = \"> \",\n   634+\n   635+    /// Render the list into the buffer at the given area.\n   636+    /// Each item takes one row. Items beyond the area height are not rendered.\n   637+    pub fn render(self: List, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   638+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n   639+        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n   640+\n   641+        const symbol_len: u16 = @intCast(@min(self.highlight_symbol.len, area.width));\n   642+        const content_start = area.x +| symbol_len;\n   643+        const content_width = area.width -| symbol_len;\n   644+\n   645+        // Render visible items\n   646+        var y = area.y;\n   647+        var item_index: usize = 0;\n   648+        while (item_index < self.items.len and y < area.bottom()) : ({\n   649+            y += 1;\n   650+            item_index += 1;\n   651+        }) {\n   652+            const item = self.items[item_index];\n   653+            const is_selected = self.selected != null and self.selected.? == item_index;\n   654+\n   655+            if (is_selected) {\n   656+                // Fill the entire row with highlight style\n   657+                const row_rect = Rect.init(area.x, y, area.width, 1);\n   658+                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n   659+\n   660+                // Draw highlight symbol\n   661+                if (symbol_len > 0) {\n   662+                    buf.setString(area.x, y, self.highlight_symbol[0..symbol_len], self.highlight_style);\n   663+                }\n   664+\n   665+                // Draw item text with highlight style\n   666+                if (content_width > 0) {\n   667+                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.highlight_style);\n   668+                }\n   669+            } else {\n   670+                // Draw item text with normal style (offset for alignment with highlighted items)\n   671+                if (content_width > 0) {\n   672+                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.style);\n   673+                }\n   674+            }\n   675+        }\n   676+    }\n   677+\n   678+    /// Get the number of items in the list\n   679+    pub fn len(self: List) usize {\n   680+        return self.items.len;\n   681+    }\n   682+\n   683+    /// Check if the list is empty\n   684+    pub fn isEmpty(self: List) bool {\n   685+        return self.items.len == 0;\n   686+    }\n   687+};\n   688+\n   689+// @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n   976+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n   977+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n   978+\n   979+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n   980+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n   981+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n   982+\n   983+/// Text alignment options\n   984+pub const Alignment = enum {\n   985+    left,\n   986+    center,\n   987+    right,\n   988+};\n   989+\n   990+/// Single-line styled text widget.\n   991+///\n   992+/// Renders text content with a given style and alignment within the provided area.\n   993+/// Text is clipped if it exceeds the available width. Only renders on the first\n   994+/// row of the area (single-line).\n   995+pub const Text = struct {\n   996+    /// The text content to display\n   997+    content: []const u8,\n   998+\n   999+    /// Style applied to the text\n  1000+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n  1001+\n  1002+    /// Text alignment within the area\n  1003+    alignment: Alignment = .left,\n  1004+\n  1005+    /// Render the text into the buffer at the given area.\n  1006+    /// Only uses the first row of the area. Text is clipped at area boundaries.\n  1007+    pub fn render(self: Text, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n  1008+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n  1009+        if (self.content.len == 0) return;\n  1010+\n  1011+        // Calculate visible text length (capped by area width)\n  1012+        const text_len = textDisplayWidth(self.content);\n  1013+        const visible_len = @min(text_len, area.width);\n  1014+\n  1015+        if (visible_len == 0) return;\n  1016+\n  1017+        // Calculate x position based on alignment\n  1018+        const x_offset: u16 = switch (self.alignment) {\n  1019+            .left => 0,\n  1020+            .center => (area.width -| visible_len) / 2,\n  1021+            .right => area.width -| visible_len,\n  1022+        };\n  1023+\n  1024+        const x = area.x +| x_offset;\n  1025+\n  1026+        // Write the text (setString handles clipping)\n  1027+        buf.setString(x, area.y, self.content, self.style);\n  1028+    }\n  1029+};\n  1030+\n  1031+/// Calculate the display width of a string (counting grapheme columns).\n  1032+/// Simple implementation: counts codepoints, treating wide chars as width 2.\n  1033+fn textDisplayWidth(str: []const u8) u16 {\n  1034+    var width: u16 = 0;\n  1035+    var iter = std.unicode.Utf8View.initUnchecked(str).iterator();\n  1036+    while (iter.nextCodepoint()) |cp| {\n  1037+        width +|= if (isWideCodepoint(cp)) 2 else 1;\n  1038+    }\n  1039+    return width;\n  1040+}\n  1041+\n  1042+/// Check if a codepoint is a wide character (CJK, etc.)\n  1043+fn isWideCodepoint(cp: u21) bool {\n  1044+    // CJK ranges (simplified)\n  1045+    return (cp >= 0x4E00 and cp <= 0x9FFF) or // CJK Unified Ideographs\n  1046+        (cp >= 0x3400 and cp <= 0x4DBF) or // CJK Extension A\n  1047+        (cp >= 0x20000 and cp <= 0x2A6DF) or // CJK Extension B\n  1048+        (cp >= 0xF900 and cp <= 0xFAFF) or // CJK Compatibility\n  1049+        (cp >= 0xFF00 and cp <= 0xFF60) or // Fullwidth forms\n  1050+        (cp >= 0xFFE0 and cp <= 0xFFE6) or // Fullwidth symbols\n  1051+        (cp >= 0x3000 and cp <= 0x303F) or // CJK Punctuation\n  1052+        (cp >= 0x1100 and cp <= 0x11FF); // Hangul Jamo\n  1053+}\n  1054+\n  1055+// ============================================================\n  1056+// SANITY TESTS - Basic Text functionality\n  1057+// ============================================================\n  1058+\n  1059+test \"sanity: Text with default values\" {\n  1060+    const text = Text{ .content = \"Hello\" };\n  1061+    try a/src/widgets/block.zig b/src/widgets/block.zig\nnew file mode 100644\nindex 0000000..fdf755f\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/src/widgets/block.zig\n@@ -0,0 +1,498 @@\n+// Block widget for zithril TUI framework\n+// Draws borders and optional title\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+const text_mod = @import(\"text.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+pub const Alignment = text_mod.Alignment;\n+\n+/// Border style variants\n+pub const BorderType = enum {\n+    none,\n+    plain, // ASCII: +-|\n+    rounded, // Unicode: rounded corners\n+    double, // Unicode: double lines\n+    thick, // Unicode: thick lines\n+\n+    /// Get the border character set for this border type\n+    pub fn chars(self: BorderType) BorderChars {\n+        return switch (self) {\n+            .none => BorderChars{\n+                .top_left = ' ',\n+                .top_right = ' ',\n+                .bottom_left = ' ',\n+                .bottom_right = ' ',\n+                .horizontal = ' ',\n+                .vertical = ' ',\n+            },\n+            .plain => BorderChars{\n+                .top_left = '+',\n+                .top_right = '+',\n+                .bottom_left = '+',\n+                .bottom_right = '+',\n+                .horizontal = '-',\n+                .vertical = '|',\n+            },\n+            .rounded => BorderChars{\n+                .top_left = 0x256D, // Box Drawings Light Arc Down and Right\n+                .top_right = 0x256E, // Box Drawings Light Arc Down and Left\n+                .bottom_left = 0x2570, // Box Drawings Light Arc Up and Right\n+                .bottom_right = 0x256F, // Box Drawings Light Arc Up and Left\n+                .horizontal = 0x2500, // Box Drawings Light Horizontal\n+                .vertical = 0x2502, // Box Drawings Light Vertical\n+            },\n+            .double => BorderChars{\n+                .top_left = 0x2554, // Box Drawings Double Down and Right\n+                .top_right = 0x2557, // Box Drawings Double Down and Left\n+                .bottom_left = 0x255A, // Box Drawings Double Up and Right\n+                .bottom_right = 0x255D, // Box Drawings Double Up and Left\n+                .horizontal = 0x2550, // Box Drawings Double Horizontal\n+                .vertical = 0x2551, // Box Drawings Double Vertical\n+            },\n+            .thick => BorderChars{\n+                .top_left = 0x250F, // Box Drawings Heavy Down and Right\n+                .top_right = 0x2513, // Box Drawings Heavy Down and Left\n+                .bottom_left = 0x2517, // Box Drawings Heavy Up and Right\n+                .bottom_right = 0x251B, // Box Drawings Heavy Up and Left\n+                .horizontal = 0x2501, // Box Drawings Heavy Horizontal\n+                .vertical = 0x2503, // Box Drawings Heavy Vertical\n+            },\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Character set for drawing borders\n+pub const BorderChars = struct {\n+    top_left: u21,\n+    top_right: u21,\n+    bottom_left: u21,\n+    bottom_right: u21,\n+    horizontal: u21,\n+    vertical: u21,\n+};\n+\n+/// Block widget that draws borders and optional title.\n+/// Use inner() on the Rect to get the interior area for child content.\n+pub const Block = struct {\n+    /// Optional title displayed at the top of the block\n+    title: ?[]const u8 = null,\n+\n+    /// Alignment of the title within the top border\n+    title_alignment: Alignment = .left,\n+\n+    /// Border style (none, plain, rounded, double, thick)\n+    border: BorderType = .none,\n+\n+    /// Style applied to border characters\n+    border_style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Background style applied to the interior of the block\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Render the block into the buffer at the given area.\n+    /// Draws the border and title, fills interior with background style.\n+    pub fn render(self: Block, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        // Fill interior with background style if we have one\n+        if (!self.style.isEmpty()) {\n+            const fill_cell = Cell.styled(' ', self.style);\n+            buf.fill(area, fill_cell);\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw border if we have one\n+        if (self.border != .none) {\n+            self.drawBorder(area, buf);\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw title if we have one\n+        if (self.title) |title| {\n+            self.drawTitle(title, area, buf);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Draw the border around the area\n+    fn drawBorder(self: Block, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        const chars = self.border.chars();\n+        const style = self.border_style;\n+\n+        const left = area.x;\n+        const right = area.right() -| 1;\n+        const top = area.y;\n+        const bottom_y = area.bottom() -| 1;\n+\n+        // Draw corners\n+        buf.set(left, top, Cell.styled(chars.top_left, style));\n+\n+        if (area.width > 1) {\n+            buf.set(right, top, Cell.styled(chars.top_right, style));\n+        }\n+\n+        if (area.height > 1) {\n+            buf.set(left, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.bottom_left, style));\n+\n+            if (area.width > 1) {\n+                buf.set(right, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.bottom_right, style));\n+            }\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw horizontal lines (top and bottom)\n+        if (area.width > 2) {\n+            const draw_bottom = area.height > 1;\n+            var x = left + 1;\n+            while (x < right) : (x += 1) {\n+                buf.set(x, top, Cell.styled(chars.horizontal, style));\n+                if (draw_bottom) {\n+                    buf.set(x, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.horizontal, style));\n+                }\n+            }\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw vertical lines (left and right sides)\n+        if (area.height > 2) {\n+            const draw_right = area.width > 1;\n+            var y = top + 1;\n+            while (y < bottom_y) : (y += 1) {\n+                buf.set(left, y, Cell.styled(chars.vertical, style));\n+                if (draw_right) {\n+                    buf.set(right, y, Cell.styled(chars.vertical, style));\n+                }\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Draw the title in the top border\n+    fn drawTitle(self: Block, title: []const u8, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        // Need at least 3 width to show any title (border + 1 char + border)\n+        if (area.width < 3) return;\n+\n+        // Calculate available space for title (inside the corners)\n+        const available_width = area.width - 2;\n+        const title_len = @min(available_width, @as(u16, @intCast(title.len)));\n+\n+        // Calculate x position based on alignment\n+        const title_x: u16 = switch (self.title_alignment) {\n+            .left => area.x + 1,\n+            .center => area.x + 1 + (available_width -| title_len) / 2,\n+            .right => area.x + 1 + (available_width -| title_len),\n+        };\n+\n+        // Draw the title with border style (title inherits border style)\n+        buf.setString(title_x, area.y, title[0..title_len], self.border_style);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the interior area (inside the border).\n+    /// Returns a Rect with margin 1 if there's a border, otherwise the full area.\n+    pub fn inner(self: Block, area: Rect) Rect {\n+        if (self.border == .none) {\n+            return area;\n+        }\n+        return area.inner(1);\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic Block functionality\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: Block with default values\" {\n+    const block = Block{};\n+    try std.testing.expect(block.title == null);\n+    try std.testing.expect(block.border == .none);\n+    try std.testing.expect(block.style.isEmpty());\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Block with title and border\" {\n+    const block = Block{\n+        .title = \"Test\",\n+        .border = .rounded,\n+    };\n+    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Test\", block.title.?);\n+    try std.testing.expect(block.border == .rounded);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Block.inner returns correct interior area\" {\n+    const block = Block{ .border = .plain };\n+    const area = Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 10);\n+    const interior = block.inner(area);\n+\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 1), interior.x);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 1), interior.y);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 18), interior.width);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 8), interior.height);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Block.inner with no border returns full area\" {\n+    const block = Block{ .border = .none };\n+    const area = std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 20), interior.width);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 10), interior.height);\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+pub const Color = style_mod.Color;\n+\n+/// Navigable list widget with items, selection highlighting, and scroll support.\n+///\n+/// Renders a vertical list of text items. The selected item is highlighted\n+/// with highlight_style and prefixed with highlight_symbol.\n+pub const List = struct {\n+    /// The items to display in the list\n+    items: []const []const u8,\n+\n+    /// Currently selected item index (null for no selection)\n+    selected: ?usize = null,\n+\n+    /// Default style for non-selected items\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Style for the selected item\n+    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n+\n+    /// Prefix shown before the selected item\n+    highlight_symbol: []const u8 = \"> \",\n+\n+    /// Render the list into the buffer at the given area.\n+    /// Each item takes one row. Items beyond the area height are not rendered.\n+    pub fn render(self: List, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n+\n+        const symbol_len: u16 = @intCast(@min(self.highlight_symbol.len, area.width));\n+        const content_start = area.x +| symbol_len;\n+        const content_width = area.width -| symbol_len;\n+\n+        // Render visible items\n+        var y = area.y;\n+        var item_index: usize = 0;\n+        while (item_index < self.items.len and y < area.bottom()) : ({\n+            y += 1;\n+            item_index += 1;\n+        }) {\n+            const item = self.items[item_index];\n+            const is_selected = self.selected != null and self.selected.? == item_index;\n+\n+            if (is_selected) {\n+                // Fill the entire row with highlight style\n+                const row_rect = Rect.init(area.x, y, area.width, 1);\n+                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n+\n+                // Draw highlight symbol\n+                if (symbol_len > 0) {\n+                    buf.setString(area.x, y, self.highlight_symbol[0..symbol_len], self.highlight_style);\n+                }\n+\n+                // Draw item text with highlight style\n+                if (content_width > 0) {\n+                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.highlight_style);\n+                }\n+            } else {\n+                // Draw item text with normal style (offset for alignment with highlighted items)\n+                if (content_width > 0) {\n+                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.style);\n+                }\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the number of items in the list\n+    pub fn len(self: List) usize {\n+        return self.items.len;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if the list is empty\n+    pub fn isEmpty(self: List) bool {\n+        return self.items.len == 0;\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic List functionality\n+// 0000000..6bc48e0\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/src/widgets/text.zig\n@@ -0,0 +1,267 @@\n+// Text widget for zithril TUI framework\n+// Single-line styled text with alignment\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+\n+/// Text alignment options\n+pub const Alignment = enum {\n+    left,\n+    center,\n+    right,\n+};\n+\n+/// Single-line styled text widget.\n+///\n+/// Renders text content with a given style and alignment within the provided area.\n+/// Text is clipped if it exceeds the available width. Only renders on the first\n+/// row of the area (single-line).\n+pub const Text = struct {\n+    /// The text content to display\n+    content: []const u8,\n+\n+    /// Style applied to the text\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Text alignment within the area\n+    alignment: Alignment = .left,\n+\n+    /// Render the text into the buffer at the given area.\n+    /// Only uses the first row of the area. Text is clipped at area boundaries.\n+    pub fn render(self: Text, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+        if (self.content.len == 0) return;\n+\n+        // Calculate visible text length (capped by area width)\n+        const text_len = textDisplayWidth(self.content);\n+        const visible_len = @min(text_len, area.width);\n+\n+        if (visible_len == 0) return;\n+\n+        // Calculate x position based on alignment\n+        const x_offset: u16 = switch (self.alignment) {\n+            .left => 0,\n+            .center => (area.width -| visible_len) / 2,\n+            .right => area.width -| visible_len,\n+        };\n+\n+        const x = area.x +| x_offset;\n+\n+        // Write the text (setString handles clipping)\n+        buf.setString(x, area.y, self.content, self.style);\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Calculate the display width of a string (counting grapheme columns).\n+/// Simple implementation: counts codepoints, treating wide chars as width 2.\n+fn textDisplayWidth(str: []const u8) u16 {\n+    var width: u16 = 0;\n+    var iter = std.unicode.Utf8View.initUnchecked(str).iterator();\n+    while (iter.nextCodepoint()) |cp| {\n+        width +|= if (isWideCodepoint(cp)) 2 else 1;\n+    }\n+    return width;\n+}\n+\n+/// Check if a codepoint is a wide character (CJK, etc.)\n+fn isWideCodepoint(cp: u21) bool {\n+    // CJK ranges (simplified)\n+    return (cp >= 0x4E00 and cp <= 0x9FFF) or // CJK Unified Ideographs\n+        (cp >= 0x3400 and cp <= 0x4DBF) or // CJK Extension A\n+        (cp >= 0x20000 and cp <= 0x2A6DF) or // CJK Extension B\n+        (cp >= 0xF900 and cp <= 0xFAFF) or // CJK Compatibility\n+        (cp >= 0xFF00 and cp <= 0xFF60) or // Fullwidth forms\n+        (cp >= 0xFFE0 and cp <= 0xFFE6) or // Fullwidth symbols\n+        (cp >= 0x3000 and cp <= 0x303F) or // CJK Punctuation\n+        (cp >= 0x1100 and cp <= 0x11FF); // Hangul Jamo\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic Text functionality\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: Text with default values\" {\n+    const text = Text{ .content = \"Hello\" };\n+    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Hello\", text.content);\n+    try std.testing.expect(text.style.isEmpty());\n+    try std.testing.expect(text.alignment == .left);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Text with custom style\" {\n+    const text = Text{\n+        .content = \"Styled\",\n+        .style = Style.init().bold().fg(.red),\n+    };\n+    try std.testing.expect(text.style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Text with alignment\" {\n+    const left = Text{ .content = \"L\", .alignment = .left };\n+    const center = Text{ .content = \"C\", .alignment = .center };\n+    const right = Text{ .content = \"R\", .alignment = .right };\n+\n+    try std.testing.expect(left.alignment == .left);\n+    try std.testing.expect(center.alignment == .center);\n+    try std.testing.expect(right.alignment == .right);\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Rendering\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text renders left-aligned\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{ .content = \"Hello\", .alignment = .left };\n+    text.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'H'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'e'), buf.get(1, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), buf.get(2, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), buf.get(3, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'o'), buf.get(4, 0).char);\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text renders center-aligned\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{ .content = \"Hi\", .alignment = .center };\n+    text.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    // \"Hi\" (2 chars) centered in 20 = offset 9\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'H'), buf.get(9, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'i'), buf.get(10, 0).char);\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text renders right-aligned\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{ .content = \"End\", .alignment = .right };\n+    text.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    // \"End\" (3 chars) right-aligned in 20 = starts at 17\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'E'), buf.get(17, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'n'), buf.get(18, 0).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'd'), buf.get(19, 0).char);\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text applies style\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{\n+        .content = \"Bold\",\n+        .style = Style.init().bold(),\n+    };\n+    text.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    try std.testing.expect(buf.get(0, 0).style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n+    try std.testing.expect(buf.get(1, 0).style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n+    try std.testing.expect(buf.get(2, 0).style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n+    try std.testing.expect(buf.get(3, 0).style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Text renders at area offset\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 30, 10);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const text = Text{ .content = \"Offset\" };\n+    text.render(Rect.init(5, 3, 10, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'O'), buf.get(5, 3).char);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, applied to the interior of the block\n    97    style: Style = Style.empty,\n    98\n    99    /// Render the block into the buffer at the given area.\n   100    /// Draws the border and title, fills interior with background style.\n   101    pub fn render(self: Block, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   102        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n   103\n   104        // Fill interior with background style if we have one\n   105        if (!self.style.isEmpty()) {\n   106            const fill_cell = Cell.styled(' ', self.style);\n   107            buf.fill(area, fill_cell);\n   108        }\n   109\n   110        // Draw border if we have one\n   111        if (self.border != .none) {\n   112            self.drawBorder(area, buf);\n   113        }\n   114\n   115        // Draw title if we have one\n   116        if (self.title) |title| {\n   117            self.drawTitle(title, area, buf);\n   118        }\n   119    }\n   120\n   121    /// Draw the border around the area\n   122    fn drawBorder(self: Block, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   123        const chars = self.border.chars();\n   124        const style = self.border_style;\n   125\n   126        const left = area.x;\n   127        const right = area.right() -| 1;\n   128        const top = area.y;\n   129        const bottom_y = area.bottom() -| 1;\n   130\n   131        // Draw corners\n   132        buf.set(left, top, Cell.styled(chars.top_left, style));\n   133\n   134        if (area.width > 1) {\n   135            buf.set(right, top, Cell.styled(chars.top_right, style));\n   136        }\n   137\n   138        if (area.height > 1) {\n   139            buf.set(left, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.bottom_left, style));\n   140\n   141            if (area.width > 1) {\n   142                buf.set(right, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.bottom_right, style));\n   143            }\n   144        }\n   145\n   146        // Draw horizontal lines (top and bottom)\n   147        if (area.width > 2) {\n   148            const draw_bottom = area.height > 1;\n   149            var x = left + 1;\n   150            while (x < right) : (x += 1) {\n   151                buf.set(x, top, Cell.styled(chars.horizontal, style));\n   152                if (draw_bottom) {\n   153                    buf.set(x, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.horizontal, style));\n   154                }\n   155            }\n   156        }\n   157\n   158        // Draw vertical lines (left and right sides)\n   159        if (area.height > 2) {\n   160            const draw_right = area.width > 1;\n   161            var y = top + 1;\n   162            while (y < bottom_y) : (y += 1) {\n   163                buf.set(left, y, Cell.styled(chars.vertical, style));\n   164                if (draw_right) {\n   165                    buf.set(right, y, Cell.styled(chars.vertical, style));\n   166                }\n   167            }\n   168        }\n   169    }\n   170\n   171    /// Draw the title in the top border\n   172    fn drawTitle(self: Block, title: []const u8, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   173        // Need at least 3 width to show any title (border + 1 char + border)\n   174        if (area.width < 3) return;\n   175\n   176        // Calculate available space for title (inside the corners)\n   177        const available_width = area.width - 2;\n   178        const title_len = @min(available_width, @as(u16, @intCast(title.len)));\n   179\n   180        // Calculate x position based on alignment\n   181        const title_x: u16 = switch (self.title_alignment) {\n   182            .left => area.x + 1,\n   183            .center => area.x + 1 + (available_width -| title_len) / 2,\n   184            .right => area.x + 1 + (available_width -| title_len),\n   185        };\n   186\n   187        // Draw the title with border style (title inherits border style)\n   188        buf.setString(title_x, area.y, title[0..title_len], self.border_style);\n   189    }\n   190\n   191    /// Get the interior area (inside the border).\n   192    /// Returns a Rect with margin 1 if there's a border, otherwise the full area.\n   193    pub fn inner(self: Block, area: Rect) Rect {\n   194        if (self.border == .none) {\n   195            return area;\n   196        }\n   197        return area.inner(1);\n   198    }\n   199};\n   200\n   201// Block widget for zithril TUI framework\n// Draws borders and optional title\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\nconst geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\nconst style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\nconst text_mod = @import(\"text.zig\");\n\npub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\npub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\npub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\npub const Style = style_mod.Style;\npub const Alignment = text_mod.Alignment;\n\n/// Border style variants\npub const BorderType = enum {\n    none,\n    plain, // ASCII: +-|\n    rounded, // Unicode: rounded corners\n    double, // Unicode: double lines\n    thick, // Unicode: thick lines\n\n    /// Get the border character set for this border type\n    pub fn chars(self: BorderType) BorderChars {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .none => BorderChars{\n                .top_left = ' ',\n                .top_right = ' ',\n                .bottom_left = ' ',\n                .bottom_right = ' ',\n                .horizontal = ' ',\n                .vertical = ' ',\n            },\n            .plain => BorderChars{\n                .top_left = '+',\n                .top_right = '+',\n                .bottom_left = '+',\n                .bottom_right = '+',\n                .horizontal = '-',\n                .vertical = '|',\n            },\n            .rounded => BorderChars{\n                .top_left = 0x256D, // Box Drawings Light Arc Down and Right\n                .top_right = 0x256E, // Box Drawings Light Arc Down and Left\n                .bottom_left = 0x2570, // Box Drawings Light Arc Up and Right\n                .bottom_right = 0x256F, // Box Drawings Light Arc Up and Left\n                .horizontal = 0x2500, // Box Drawings Light Horizontal\n                .vertical = 0x2502, // Box Drawings Light Vertical\n            },\n            .double => BorderChars{\n                .top_left = 0x2554, // Box Drawings Double Down and Right\n                .top_right = 0x2557, // Box Drawings Double Down and Left\n                .bottom_left = 0x255A, // Box Drawings Double Up and Right\n                .bottom_right = 0x255D, // Box Drawings Double Up and Left\n                .horizontal = 0x2550, // Box Drawings Double Horizontal\n                .vertical = 0x2551, // Box Drawings Double Vertical\n            },\n            .thick => BorderChars{\n                .top_left = 0x250F, // Box Drawings Heavy Down and Right\n                .top_right = 0x2513, // Box Drawings Heavy Down and Left\n                .bottom_left = 0x2517, // Box Drawings Heavy Up and Right\n                .bottom_right = 0x251B, // Box Drawings Heavy Up and Left\n                .horizontal = 0x2501, // Box Drawings Heavy Horizontal\n                .vertical = 0x2503, // Box Drawings Heavy Vertical\n            },\n        };\n    }\n};\n\n/// Character set for drawing borders\npub const BorderChars = struct {\n    top_left: u21,\n    top_right: u21,\n    bottom_left: u21,\n    bottom_right: u21,\n    horizontal: u21,\n    vertical: u21,\n};\n\n/// Block widget that draws borders and optional title.\n/// Use inner() on the Rect to get the interior area for child content.\npub const Block = struct {\n    /// Optional title displayed at the top of the block\n    title: ?[]const u8 = null,\n\n    /// Alignment of the title within the top border\n    title_alignment: Alignment = .left,\n\n    /// Border style (none, plain, rounded, double, thick)\n    border: BorderType = .none,\n\n    /// Style applied to border characters\n    border_style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Background style applied to the interior of the block\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Render the block into the buffer at the given area.\n    /// Draws the border and title, fills interior with background style.\n    pub fn render(self: Block, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        // Fill interior with background style if we have one\n        if (!self.style.isEmpty()) {\n            const fill_cell = Cell.styled(' ', self.style);\n            buf.fill(area, fill_cell);\n        }\n\n        // Draw border if we have one\n        if (self.border != .none) {\n            self.drawBorder(area, buf);\n        }\n\n        // Draw title if we have one\n        if (self.title) |title| {\n            self.drawTitle(title, area, buf);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Draw the border around the area\n    fn drawBorder(self: Block, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        const chars = self.border.chars();\n        const style = self.border_style;\n\n        const left = area.x;\n        const right = area.right() -| 1;\n        const top = area.y;\n        const bottom_y = area.bottom() -| 1;\n\n        // Draw corners\n        buf.set(left, top, Cell.styled(chars.top_left, style));\n\n        if (area.width > 1) {\n            buf.set(right, top, Cell.styled(chars.top_right, style));\n        }\n\n        if (area.height > 1) {\n            buf.set(left, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.bottom_left, style));\n\n            if (area.width > 1) {\n                buf.set(right, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.bottom_right, style));\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Draw horizontal lines (top and bottom)\n        if (area.width > 2) {\n            const draw_bottom = area.height > 1;\n            var x = left + 1;\n            while (x < right) : (x += 1) {\n                buf.set(x, top, Cell.styled(chars.horizontal, style));\n                if (draw_bottom) {\n                    buf.set(x, bottom_y, Cell.styled(chars.horizontal, style));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Draw vertical lines (left and right sides)\n        if (area.height > 2) {\n            const draw_right = area.width > 1;\n            var y = top + 1;\n            while (y < bottom_y) : (y += 1) {\n                buf.set(left, y, Cell.styled(chars.vertical, style));\n                if (draw_right) {\n                    buf.set(right, y, Cell.styled(chars.vertical, style));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Draw the title in the top border\n    fn drawTitle(self: Block, title: []const u8, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        // Need at least 3 width to show any title (border + 1 char + border)\n        if (area.width < 3) return;\n\n        // Calculate available space for title (inside the corners)\n        const available_width = area.width - 2;\n        const title_len = @min(available_width, @as(u16, @intCast(title.len)));\n\n        // Calculate x position based on alignment\n        const title_x: u16 = switch (self.title_alignment) {\n            .left => area.x + 1,\n            .center => area.x + 1 + (available_width -| title_len) / 2,\n            .right => area.x + 1 + (available_width -| title_len),\n        };\n\n        // Draw the title with border style (title inherits border style)\n        buf.setString(title_x, area.y, title[0..title_len], self.border_style);\n    }\n\n    /// Get the interior area (inside the border).\n    /// Returns a Rect with margin 1 if there's a border, otherwise the full area.\n    pub fn inner(self: Block, area: Rect) Rect {\n        if (self.border == .none) {\n            return area;\n        }\n        return area.inner(1);\n    }\n};\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic Only renders on the first\n    24/// row of the area (single-line).\n    25pub const Text = struct {\n    26    /// The text content to display\n    27    content: []const u8,\n    28\n    29    /// Style applied to the text\n    30    style: Style = Style.empty,\n    31\n    32    /// Text alignment within the area\n    33    alignment: Alignment = .left,\n    34\n    35    /// Render the text into the buffer at the given area.\n    36    /// Only uses the first row of the area. Text is clipped at area boundaries.\n    37    pub fn render(self: Text, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n    38        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n    39        if (self.content.len == 0) return;\n    40\n    41        // Calculate visible text length (capped by area width)\n    42        const text_len = textDisplayWidth(self.content);\n    43        const visible_len = @min(text_len, area.width);\n    44\n    45        if (visible_len == 0) return;\n    46\n    47        // Calculate x position based on alignment\n    48        const x_offset: u16 = switch (self.alignment) {\n    49            .left => 0,\n    50            .center => (area.width -| visible_len) / 2,\n    51            .right => area.width -| visible_len,\n    52        };\n    53\n    54        const x = area.x +| x_offset;\n    55\n    56        // Write the text (setString handles clipping)\n    57        buf.setString(x, area.y, self.content, self.style);\n    58    }\n    59};\n    60\n    61/// Calculate the display width of a string (counting grapheme columns).\n    62/// Simple implementation: counts codepoints, treating wide chars as width 2.\n    63fn textDisplayWidth(str: []const u8) u16 {\n    64    var width: u16 = 0;\n    65    var iter = std.unicode.Utf8View.initUnchecked(str).iterator();\n    66    while (iter.nextCodepoint()) |cp| {\n    67        width +|= if (isWideCodepoint(cp)) 2 else 1;\n    68    }\n    69    return width;\n    70}\n    71\n    72/// Check if a codepoint is a wide character (CJK, etc.)\n    73fn isWideCodepoint(cp: u21) bool {\n    74    // CJK ranges (simplified)\n    75    return (cp >= 0x4E00 and cp <= 0x9FFF) or // CJK Unified Ideographs\n    76        (cp >= 0x3400 and cp <= 0x4DBF) or // CJK Extension A\n    77        (cp >= 0x20000 and cp <= 0x2A6DF) or // CJK Extension B\n    78        (cp >= 0xF900 and cp <= 0xFAFF) or // CJK Compatibility\n    79        (cp >= 0xFF00 and cp <= 0xFF60) or // Fullwidth forms\n    80        (cp >= 0xFFE0 and cp <= 0xFFE6) or // Fullwidth symbols\n    81        (cp >= 0x3000 and cp <= 0x303F) or // CJK Punctuation\n    82        (cp >= 0x1100 and cp <= 0x11FF); // Hangul Jamo\n    83}\n    84\n    85// ============================================================\n    86// SANITY TESTS - Basic Text functionality\n    87// ============================================================\n    88\n    89test \"sanity: Text with default values\" {\n    90    const text = Text{ .content = \"Hello\" };\n    91    try 96test \"sanity: Text with custom style\" {\n    97    const text = Text{\n    98        .content = \"Styled\",\n    99        .style = Style.init().bold().fg(.red),\n   100    };\n   101    try .left);\n   110    try std.testing.expect(center.alignment == .center);\n   111    try std.testing.expect(right.alignment == .right);\n   112}\n   113\n   114// ============================================================\n   115// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Rendering\n   116// ============================================================\n   117\n   118test \"behavior: Text renders left-aligned\" {\n   119    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n   120    defer buf.deinit();\n   121\n   122    const text = Text{ .content = \"Hello\", .alignment 3);\n   134    defer buf.deinit();\n   135\n   136    const text = Text{ .content = \"Hi\", .alignment = .center };\n   137    text.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n   138\n   139    // \"Hi\" Text is clipped at area boundaries.\n    pub fn render(self: Text, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n        if (self.content.len == 0) return;\n\n        // self.content, self.style);\n    }\n};\n\n/// Calculate the display width of a string (counting grapheme columns).\n/// Simple implementation: counts codepoints, treating wide chars as width 2.\nfn textDisplayWidth(str: []const u8) u16 {\n    var width: u16 = 0;\n    var iter = std.unicode.Utf8View.initUnchecked(str).iterator();\n    while (iter.nextCodepoint()) |cp| {\n        width +|= if (isWideCodepoint(cp)) 2 else 1;\n    }\n    return width;\n}\n\n/// Check if a codepoint is a wide character (CJK, etc.)\nfn isWideCodepoint(cp: u21) bool {\n    // CJK ranges (simplified)\n    return (cp >= 0x4E00 and cp <= 0x9FFF) or // CJK Unified Ideographs\n        (cp >= 0x3400 and cp <= 0x4DBF) or // CJK Extension A\n        (cp >= 0x20000 and cp <= 0x2A6DF) or // CJK Extension B\n             const row_rect = Rect.init(area.x, y, area.width, 1);\n    58                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n    59\n    60                // Draw highlight The selected item is highlighted\n/// with highlight_style and prefixed with highlight_symbol.\npub const List = struct {\n    /// The items to display in the list\n    items: []const []const u8,\n\n    /// Currently selected item index (null for no selection)\n    selected: ?usize = null,\n\n    /// Default style for non-selected items\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Style for the selected item\n    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n\n    /// Prefix shown before the selected item\n    highlight_symbol: []const u8 = \"> \",\n\n    /// Render the list into the buffer at the given area.\n    /// Each item takes one row. Items beyond the area height are not rendered.\n    pub fn render(self: List, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n\n        const symbol_len: u16 = @intCast(@min(self.highlight_symbol.len, area.width));\n        const content_start = area.x +| symbol_len;\n        const content_width = area.width -| symbol_len;\n\n        // Render visible items\n        var y = area.y;\n        var item_index: usize = 0;\n        while (item_index < self.items.len and y < area.bottom()) : ({\n            y += 1;\n            item_index += 1;\n        }) {\n            const item = self.items[item_index];\n            const is_selected = self.selected != null and self.selected.? == item_index;\n\n            if (is_selected) {\n                // Fill the entire row with highlight style\n                const row_rect = Rect.init(area.x, y, area.width, 1);\n                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n\n                // Draw highlight symbol\n                if (symbol_len > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(area.x, y, self.highlight_symbol[0..symbol_len], self.highlight_style);\n                }\n\n                // Draw item text with highlight style\n                if (content_width > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.highlight_style);\n                }\n            } else {\n                // Draw item text with normal style (offset for alignment with highlighted items)\n                if (content_width > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.style);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of items in the list\n    pub fn len(self: List) usize {\n        return self.items.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if the list is empty\n    pub fn isEmpty(self: List) bool {\n        return self.items.len == 0;\n    }\n};\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic List functionality\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: List with default values\" {\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\", \"c\" };\n    const list = List{ .items = &items };\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), list.len());\n    try std.testing.expect(list.selected == null);\n    try std.testing.expect(list.style.isEmpty());\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"> \", list.highlight_symbol);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: List with null);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 1), list.selected.?);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: List with custom styles\" {\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\" };\n    const list = List{\n std.testing.expect(!list.style.isEmpty());\n    try std.testing.expect(list.highlight_style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"* \", list.highlight_symbol);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: List.len and List.isEmpty\" {\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\" };\n    const list = List{ .items = &items };\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), list.len());\n ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: List renders items\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n highlight_symbol length (2)\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'A'), buf.get(2, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), buf.get(3, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'B'), buf.get(2, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'G'), buf.get(2, 2).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: List renders selected item with highlight\" {\n The selected item is highlighted\n/// with highlight_style and prefixed with highlight_symbol.\npub const List = struct {\n    /// The items to display in the list\n    items: []const []const u8,\n\n    /// Currently selected item index (null for no selection)\n    selected: ?usize = null,\n\n    /// Default style for non-selected items\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Style for the selected item\n    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n\n    /// Prefix shown before the selected item\n    highlight_symbol: []const u8 = \"> \",\n\n    /// Render the list into the buffer at the given area.\n    /// Each item takes one row. Items beyond the area height are not rendered.\n    pub fn render(self: List, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n\n        const symbol_len: u16 = @intCast(@min(self.highlight_symbol.len, area.width));\n        const content_start = area.x +| symbol_len;\n        const content_width = area.width -| symbol_len;\n\n        // Render visible items\n        var y = area.y;\n        var item_index: usize = 0;\n        while (item_index < self.items.len and y < area.bottom()) : ({\n            y += 1;\n            item_index += 1;\n        }) {\n            const item = self.items[item_index];\n            const is_selected = self.selected != null and self.selected.? == item_index;\n\n            if (is_selected) {\n                // Fill the entire row with highlight style\n                const row_rect = Rect.init(area.x, y, area.width, 1);\n                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n\n                // Draw highlight symbol\n                if (symbol_len > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(area.x, y, self.highlight_symbol[0..symbol_len], self.highlight_style);\n                }\n\n                // Draw item text with highlight style\n                if (content_width > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.highlight_style);\n                }\n            } else {\n                // Draw item text with normal style (offset for alignment with highlighted items)\n                if (content_width > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.style);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of items in the list\n    pub fn len(self: List) usize {\n        return self.items.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if the list is empty\n    pub fn isEmpty(self: List) bool {\n        return self.items.len == 0;\n    }\n};\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic List functionality\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: List with default values\" {\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\", \"c\" };\n    const list = List{ .items = &items };\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), list.len());\n    try std.testing.expect(list.selected == null);\n    try std.testing.expect(list.style.isEmpty());\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"> \", list.highlight_symbol);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: List with null);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 1), list.selected.?);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: List with custom styles\" {\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\" };\n    const list = List{\n \"sanity: List.len and List.isEmpty\" {\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\" };\n    const list = List{ .items = &items };\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), list.len());\n ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: List renders items\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n
